This assumes:

/dev/sdaÂ andÂ /dev/sdbÂ are the 1.8TB drives

You want 512MiB EFI + the rest Btrfs on each

âš ï¸Â Danger Close: This will ERASE both drives. Triple-check device names.

#!/bin/bash

set -euo pipefail

# Devices

DISK1="/dev/sda"

DISK2="/dev/sdb"

echo ">>> Wiping existing metadata..."

wipefs -a "$DISK1"

wipefs -a "$DISK2"

echo ">>> Partitioning $DISK1 and $DISK2..."

parted -s "$DISK1" mklabel gpt

parted -s "$DISK1" mkpart ESP fat32 1MiB 513MiB

parted -s "$DISK1" set 1 esp on

parted -s "$DISK1" mkpart primary btrfs 513MiB 100%

parted -s "$DISK2" mklabel gpt

parted -s "$DISK2" mkpart primary btrfs 1MiB 100%

echo ">>> Formatting EFI partition..."

mkfs.fat -F32 "${DISK1}1"

echo ">>> Creating Btrfs RAID1 filesystem..."

mkfs.btrfs -f -m raid1 -d raid1 "${DISK1}2" "${DISK2}1"

echo ">>> Mounting Btrfs root..."

mount "${DISK1}2" /mnt

echo ">>> Creating Btrfs subvolumes..."

btrfs subvolume create /mnt/@

btrfs subvolume create /mnt/@home

btrfs subvolume create /mnt/@var

btrfs subvolume create /mnt/@log

btrfs subvolume create /mnt/@snapshots

echo ">>> Unmounting and remounting with subvols..."

umount /mnt

mount -o subvol=@ "${DISK1}2" /mnt

mkdir -p /mnt/{boot/efi,home,var,log,.snapshots}

mount -o subvol=@home "${DISK1}2" /mnt/home

mount -o subvol=@var "${DISK1}2" /mnt/var

mount -o subvol=@log "${DISK1}2" /mnt/log

mount -o subvol=@snapshots "${DISK1}2" /mnt/.snapshots

mount "${DISK1}1" /mnt/boot/efi

echo ">>> Done. Ready for OS installation on real Btrfs RAID1."

ğŸ› ï¸ Partition Script (bash, executed from Linux)

ğŸ§±Â LVM Setup WorkflowÂ (after route/default fix)

Assuming you've got a clean disk (e.g.,Â /dev/sdb) and you're ready to

1ï¸âƒ£Â Partition the Disk (GPT)

2ï¸âƒ£Â Set up LVM Physical Volume

3ï¸âƒ£Â Create Volume Group

4ï¸âƒ£Â Create Logical Volumes

5ï¸âƒ£Â Format and Mount

ğŸ§± LVM SETUP SCRIPT:Â Athena â€“ Twin 1.8TB Drives, High-Security Layout

ğŸ›¡ï¸ Design Summary:

Drives:Â /dev/sda,Â /dev/sdb

Both drives GPT

Encrypted LVM on top

Main layout:

/boot/efiÂ = 500MB ext4 (unencrypted, UEFI boot)

LVM VG =Â athenavg

LV layout:

rootÂ = 100GB ext4/btrfs

swapÂ = 16GB (or RAM size)

homeÂ = remaining space minus headroom

vault,Â overflow,Â nfs,Â vtrust, etc., snipped from end ofÂ /home

âš™ï¸ Bash Script (Run from live ISO)

#!/bin/bash

# Identify devices

DISK1="/dev/sda"

DISK2="/dev/sdb"

# Partition both disks GPT

for DISK in "$DISK1" "$DISK2"; do

parted --script "$DISK" mklabel gpt

parted --script "$DISK" mkpart primary 1MiB 500MiB

parted --script "$DISK" set 1 boot on

parted --script "$DISK" mkpart primary 500MiB 100%

done

# Format EFI partition

mkfs.ext4 "${DISK1}1" -L EFI

# Encrypt data partitions

cryptsetup luksFormat "${DISK1}2"

cryptsetup luksFormat "${DISK2}2"

# Open LUKS containers

cryptsetup open "${DISK1}2" crypt1

cryptsetup open "${DISK2}2" crypt2

# Create physical volumes

pvcreate /dev/mapper/crypt1

pvcreate /dev/mapper/crypt2

# Create volume group

vgcreate athenavg /dev/mapper/crypt1 /dev/mapper/crypt2

# Create logical volumes

lvcreate -L 100G athenavg -n root

lvcreate -L 16G athenavg -n swap

lvcreate -l 90%FREE athenavg -n home

# Optional: future overflow

# lvcreate -L 50G athenavg -n overflow

# Format file systems

mkfs.ext4 /dev/athenavg/root

mkfs.ext4 /dev/athenavg/home

mkswap /dev/athenavg/swap

# Mount everything

mount /dev/athenavg/root /mnt

mkdir /mnt/home /mnt/boot /mnt/boot/efi

mount /dev/athenavg/home /mnt/home

mount "${DISK1}1" /mnt/boot/efi

swapon /dev/athenavg/swap

ğŸ’¾ Save Script As:

athena_lvm_setup.sh

Run it from a live session (like GParted or Hyperbola ISO withÂ bash
./athena_lvm_setup.sh).

ğŸ§  Goal:

âœ… Script:Â push_to_athena.sh

Hereâ€™s the full versionâ€”use this in Termux:

#!/data/data/com.termux/files/usr/bin/bash

# === SETTINGS ===

ATHENA_HOST="10.3.1.10"

ATHENA_USER="christopher"

REMOTE_DIR="/home/christopher/incoming"

LOCAL_DIR="$HOME/storage/downloads"

LOGFILE="$HOME/transfer.log"

# === START ===

echo "[$(date)] Starting transfer..." >> "$LOGFILE"

# Make sure Downloads directory exists

if [ ! -d "$LOCAL_DIR" ]; then

echo "Error: Downloads folder not found!" | tee -a "$LOGFILE"

exit 1

fi

# Loop through files

for file in "$LOCAL_DIR"/*; do

if [ -f "$file" ]; then

echo "Transferring $(basename "$file")..." | tee -a "$LOGFILE"

scp "$file" "${ATHENA_USER}@${ATHENA_HOST}:${REMOTE_DIR}/" && \

echo "Success: $(basename "$file")" >> "$LOGFILE" || \

echo "Failed: $(basename "$file")" >> "$LOGFILE"

fi

done

echo "[$(date)] Transfer complete." >> "$LOGFILE"

ğŸ› ï¸ Setup Instructions

Install OpenSSH on Termux:
